   `covered_entity_ids` = ⋃ over the 4-role audit rows of `covered_element_ids` — i.e. the EXACT
   set the 4-role seam already computed via `_claim_covers_entity` (the operator-locked
   exact-canonical-match authority). The ledger NEVER sets is_verified, NEVER re-implements
   coverage matching, NEVER adds a credit path. Confirm `manifest["required_entity_coverage"]`
   cannot change the D8 release decision (it is written AFTER the seam's release decision and is
   not read by any gate).
2. **Gaps disclosed, NEVER filled.** A GAP_DISCLOSED slot becomes a deterministic templated
   "could not verify X" sentence (no LLM, no fabricated citation). Confirm there is no path where
   a gap is filled with an unsupported claim.

   reconciliation are all unchanged. The Coverage gaps section is appended AFTER the redaction +
   V30 disclosure (so it reflects the final shipped body), is ADDITIVE disclosure (not a claim in
   the body), and so is not subject to (and does not interfere with) the redaction pass.
4. **Default-OFF byte-identical.** `PG_REQUIRED_ENTITY_LEDGER` read at call time; OFF -> the whole
   block is skipped -> report.md + manifest byte-identical. Confirm.
5. **Fail-soft.** The block is wrapped try/except -> a failure logs + continues, NEVER aborts the
   run (a disclosure surface must not break a paid run). Confirm it cannot crash the run.
6. **Native-template-only (contamination lock).** Required entities come from
   `load_required_entities(_template, q["slug"])` (the native scope template); the block NEVER
   reads `outputs/dr_benchmark/`. Confirm.

+"""I-perm-021 (#1213) — RequiredEntityLedger: report-level required-entity completeness
+accounting + honest gap disclosure (Codex design-gate APPROVE; narrow scope).
+
+The completeness gap is largely UPSTREAM (retrieval/extraction); a reduce-time/report-level
+ledger CANNOT manufacture coverage. Its job, per the Codex design ruling, is the NARROW
+"inclusion + disclosure" surface (NO second LLM generation / recovery round — that is a
+deferred follow-up):
+
+  - Phase B (THIS module, report-level, POST-strict_verify): given the pre-registered native
+    `required_entities` and the set of entity ids that earned a VERIFIED binding (the UNION of
+    every VERIFIED claim's ``covered_element_ids`` from
+    ``native_gate_b_inputs.build_native_gate_b_inputs`` — the EXACT same coverage computation,
+    reused, never re-implemented), mark each required slot VERIFIED or GAP_DISCLOSED and emit
+    an HONEST, DETERMINISTIC, TEMPLATED disclosure (no LLM, no fabricated citation).
+
+§-1.1 SAFETY: this module assigns NO verdicts and adds NO coverage CREDIT. VERIFIED is set
+ONLY from the caller's already-computed verified-binding set (which is itself gated by
+strict_verify + the 4-role ``verdict==VERIFIED`` rule). It never touches strict_verify / the
+4-role evaluator / D8 / the release decision. A gap disclosure is a templated "we could not
+verify X" statement — it NEVER fills the gap with an unsupported claim.
+
+Required entities come ONLY from the native scope template (the contamination lock — never
+``outputs/dr_benchmark/`` / the gold rubric). The caller reads ``PG_REQUIRED_ENTITY_LEDGER``
+at CALL TIME (default OFF, byte-identical when off); this pure module is simply not invoked
+when the flag is off.
+"""
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+from dataclasses import dataclass, field
+
+# ── slot state machine ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
+# (Phase A states RETRIEVED/MAPPED are produced by the pre-gen retrieval feed, a separate PR;
+#  this narrow disclosure module uses only the post-verify VERIFIED / GAP_DISCLOSED transition.)
+STATE_MISSING = "missing"
+STATE_RETRIEVED = "retrieved"
+STATE_MAPPED = "mapped"
+STATE_VERIFIED = "verified"
+STATE_INCLUDED = "included"
+STATE_GAP_DISCLOSED = "gap_disclosed"
+
+# native required-entity dict keys (mirrors native_gate_b_inputs; read-only here).
+_KEY_ID = "id"
+_KEY_SEVERITY = "severity"
+_KEY_ANCHOR = "anchor"
+_KEY_RENDERING_SLOT = "rendering_slot"
+_KEY_S0_CATEGORY = "s0_category"
+# canonical identifier keys, in disclosure-preference order.
+_CANONICAL_KEYS = ("doi", "pmid", "url_pattern")
+
+
+@dataclass
+class RequiredSlot:
+    """One required entity's completeness state + the metadata needed to disclose it."""
+    entity_id: str
+    severity: str
+    s0_category: str | None
+    anchor: str
+    rendering_slot: str
+    canonical_ids: dict           # {doi?, pmid?, url_pattern?} (only present keys)
+    state: str
+    note: str = ""                # disclosure qualifier (e.g. url_mismatch); never a claim
+
+    @property
+    def is_url_pattern_only(self) -> bool:
+        """True iff url_pattern is the ENTITY's only canonical id (no doi/pmid). Such an
+        entity is structurally un-flippable by alternate-URL retrieval — coverage requires the
+        VERIFIED claim to cite the exact canonical url_pattern (Codex design-gate q7)."""
+        return "url_pattern" in self.canonical_ids and not (
+            self.canonical_ids.get("doi") or self.canonical_ids.get("pmid")
+        )
+
+
+# Disclosure qualifier (Codex design-gate q7): public-facing, NOT raw internal artifact wording.
+_URL_MISMATCH_NOTE = (
+    "content for this topic may exist on an alternate source, but coverage remains unmet "
+    "unless a verified claim cites the canonical source for this required entity"
+)
+
+
+@dataclass
+class RequiredEntityLedger:
+    slots: list[RequiredSlot] = field(default_factory=list)
+
+    def verified_slots(self) -> list[RequiredSlot]:
+        return [s for s in self.slots if s.state in (STATE_VERIFIED, STATE_INCLUDED)]
+
+    def gap_slots(self) -> list[RequiredSlot]:
+        return [s for s in self.slots if s.state == STATE_GAP_DISCLOSED]
+
+    def coverage_fraction(self) -> float:
+        return (len(self.verified_slots()) / len(self.slots)) if self.slots else 0.0
+
+    def to_evidence_gaps(self) -> list[dict]:
+        """Structured gap records for the manifest (machine-readable, audit trail)."""
+        return [
+            {
+                "entity_id": s.entity_id,
+                "severity": s.severity,
+                "s0_category": s.s0_category,
+                "anchor": s.anchor,
+                "rendering_slot": s.rendering_slot,
+                "reason": "no_verified_citation",
+                "note": s.note,
+            }
+            for s in self.gap_slots()
+        ]
+
+
+def _canonical_ids(entity: dict) -> dict:
+    return {k: entity[k] for k in _CANONICAL_KEYS if entity.get(k) not in (None, "")}
+
+
+def build_ledger(
+    required_entities: list[dict],
+    covered_entity_ids: set[str] | frozenset[str] | list[str],
+) -> RequiredEntityLedger:
+    """Phase B: build the report-level ledger from the native required entities + the
+    VERIFIED-binding set (``⋃ verified_claim.covered_element_ids``, computed by
+    ``native_gate_b_inputs``). A required entity is VERIFIED iff its id is in
+    ``covered_entity_ids`` (the exact existing coverage authority), else GAP_DISCLOSED.
+    Assigns NO new credit; this is pure accounting + disclosure over an already-decided set."""
+    covered = set(covered_entity_ids)
+    slots: list[RequiredSlot] = []
+    for entity in required_entities:
+        entity_id = entity.get(_KEY_ID)
+        if entity_id in (None, ""):
+            # a config error elsewhere (validate_entity_severity is the fail-loud guard); skip
+            # defensively here so the ledger never crashes on a malformed slot.
+            continue
+        canonical_ids = _canonical_ids(entity)
+        verified = entity_id in covered
+        slot = RequiredSlot(
+            entity_id=str(entity_id),
+            severity=str(entity.get(_KEY_SEVERITY, "")),
+            s0_category=entity.get(_KEY_S0_CATEGORY),
+            anchor=str(entity.get(_KEY_ANCHOR, "")),
+            rendering_slot=str(entity.get(_KEY_RENDERING_SLOT, "")),
+            canonical_ids=canonical_ids,
+            state=STATE_VERIFIED if verified else STATE_GAP_DISCLOSED,
+        )
+        if not verified and slot.is_url_pattern_only:
+            slot.note = _URL_MISMATCH_NOTE
+        slots.append(slot)
+    return RequiredEntityLedger(slots=slots)
+
+
+def render_coverage_gaps_section(ledger: RequiredEntityLedger) -> str:
+    """Deterministic, public-facing 'Coverage gaps' report section (NO LLM, NO fabricated
+    citation, NO raw internal artifact wording — Codex design-gate q5 + P2). Returns "" when
+    there are no gaps so the section is omitted entirely (and the OFF path stays byte-identical)."""
+    gaps = ledger.gap_slots()
+    if not gaps:
+        return ""
+    lines = [
+        "## Coverage gaps",
+        "",
+        "The following pre-registered required topics could not be supported by a verified "
+        "citation in this report. They are disclosed here rather than asserted without "
+        "evidence:",
+        "",
+    ]
+    for s in gaps:
+        label = s.anchor or s.entity_id
+        sev = f" ({s.severity})" if s.severity else ""
+        note = f" — {s.note}" if s.note else ""
+        lines.append(f"- **{label}**{sev}: not verified in this run{note}.")
+    lines.append("")
+    return "\n".join(lines)

+"""I-perm-021 (#1213) — RequiredEntityLedger (narrow: inclusion + honest disclosure).
+
+Proves the ledger is pure accounting + honest disclosure over the ALREADY-computed
+verified-binding set: VERIFIED only when the entity id is in the covered set (no new credit),
+GAP_DISCLOSED otherwise; url_pattern-only missing entities get the canonical-mismatch note;
+the Coverage gaps section is deterministic public prose (no LLM, no fabricated citation) and
+EMPTY when there are no gaps (so the OFF path stays byte-identical).
+"""
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+from src.polaris_graph.generator.required_entity_ledger import (
+    STATE_GAP_DISCLOSED,
+    STATE_VERIFIED,
+    build_ledger,
+    render_coverage_gaps_section,
+)
+
+
+def _ent(eid, *, severity="S1", anchor="", rendering_slot="", **canon):
+    e = {"id": eid, "severity": severity, "anchor": anchor, "rendering_slot": rendering_slot}
+    e.update(canon)
+    return e
+
+
+def test_verified_and_gap_states():
+    entities = [
+        _ent("e1", doi="10.1/a", anchor="Trial A"),
+        _ent("e2", doi="10.1/b", anchor="Trial B"),
+        _ent("e3", pmid="123", anchor="Trial C"),
+    ]
+    led = build_ledger(entities, covered_entity_ids={"e1", "e3"})
+    by = {s.entity_id: s for s in led.slots}
+    assert by["e1"].state == STATE_VERIFIED
+    assert by["e3"].state == STATE_VERIFIED
+    assert by["e2"].state == STATE_GAP_DISCLOSED
+    assert {s.entity_id for s in led.verified_slots()} == {"e1", "e3"}
+    assert {s.entity_id for s in led.gap_slots()} == {"e2"}
+    assert round(led.coverage_fraction(), 4) == round(2 / 3, 4)
+
+
+def test_no_new_credit_a_missing_entity_stays_gap():
+    # §-1.1: the ledger never flips a slot to VERIFIED unless its id is in the covered set.
+    entities = [_ent("e1", doi="10.1/a")]
+    assert build_ledger(entities, covered_entity_ids=set()).slots[0].state == STATE_GAP_DISCLOSED
+    assert build_ledger(entities, covered_entity_ids={"e1"}).slots[0].state == STATE_VERIFIED
+
+
+def test_url_pattern_only_gap_gets_mismatch_note_but_doi_gap_does_not():
+    entities = [
+        _ent("u1", url_pattern="https://fda.gov/label/x", anchor="FDA label X"),
+        _ent("d1", doi="10.1/d", url_pattern="https://x", anchor="Trial D"),  # has doi too
+    ]
+    led = build_ledger(entities, covered_entity_ids=set())
+    by = {s.entity_id: s for s in led.slots}
+    assert by["u1"].note and "canonical source" in by["u1"].note   # url_pattern-only -> note
+    assert by["d1"].note == ""                                      # doi-bearing -> no note
+
+
+def test_evidence_gaps_records():
+    entities = [_ent("e2", severity="S0", s0_category="contraindications", anchor="X")]
+    led = build_ledger(entities, covered_entity_ids=set())
+    gaps = led.to_evidence_gaps()
+    assert len(gaps) == 1
+    g = gaps[0]
+    assert g["entity_id"] == "e2" and g["severity"] == "S0"
+    assert g["s0_category"] == "contraindications" and g["reason"] == "no_verified_citation"
+
+
+def test_coverage_gaps_section_empty_when_no_gaps():
+    entities = [_ent("e1", doi="10.1/a")]
+    led = build_ledger(entities, covered_entity_ids={"e1"})
+    assert render_coverage_gaps_section(led) == ""   # byte-identical OFF/no-gap path
+
+
+def test_coverage_gaps_section_is_public_prose_no_internal_wording():
+    entities = [
+        _ent("e2", anchor="Trial B", doi="10.1/b"),
+        _ent("u1", anchor="FDA label X", url_pattern="https://fda.gov/x"),
+    ]
+    led = build_ledger(entities, covered_entity_ids=set())
+    out = render_coverage_gaps_section(led)
+    assert out.startswith("## Coverage gaps")
+    assert "Trial B" in out and "FDA label X" in out
+    assert "not verified in this run" in out
+    assert "canonical source" in out                  # the url_pattern note surfaces
+    # no raw internal artifact-path wording (Codex design-gate P2)
+    for banned in ("FRAME_GAP", "compose_gap_payload", "_GAP_STUB", "kept_sentences",
+                   "strict_verify", "evidence_id"):
+        assert banned not in out
+    # NEVER fills a gap with a claim — it only discloses absence
+    assert "verified citation" in out


 succeeded in 8553ms:
"""I-perm-021 (#1213) — RequiredEntityLedger (narrow: inclusion + honest disclosure).

Proves the ledger is pure accounting + honest disclosure over the ALREADY-computed
verified-binding set: VERIFIED only when the entity id is in the covered set (no new credit),
GAP_DISCLOSED otherwise; url_pattern-only missing entities get the canonical-mismatch note;
the Coverage gaps section is deterministic public prose (no LLM, no fabricated citation) and
EMPTY when there are no gaps (so the OFF path stays byte-identical).
"""
from __future__ import annotations

from src.polaris_graph.generator.required_entity_ledger import (
    STATE_GAP_DISCLOSED,
    STATE_VERIFIED,
    build_ledger,
    render_coverage_gaps_section,
)


def _ent(eid, *, severity="S1", anchor="", rendering_slot="", **canon):
    e = {"id": eid, "severity": severity, "anchor": anchor, "rendering_slot": rendering_slot}
    e.update(canon)
    return e


def test_verified_and_gap_states():
    entities = [
        _ent("e1", doi="10.1/a", anchor="Trial A"),
        _ent("e2", doi="10.1/b", anchor="Trial B"),
        _ent("e3", pmid="123", anchor="Trial C"),
    ]
    led = build_ledger(entities, covered_entity_ids={"e1", "e3"})
    by = {s.entity_id: s for s in led.slots}
    assert by["e1"].state == STATE_VERIFIED
    assert by["e3"].state == STATE_VERIFIED
    assert by["e2"].state == STATE_GAP_DISCLOSED
    assert {s.entity_id for s in led.verified_slots()} == {"e1", "e3"}
    assert {s.entity_id for s in led.gap_slots()} == {"e2"}
    assert round(led.coverage_fraction(), 4) == round(2 / 3, 4)


def test_no_new_credit_a_missing_entity_stays_gap():
    # §-1.1: the ledger never flips a slot to VERIFIED unless its id is in the covered set.
    entities = [_ent("e1", doi="10.1/a")]
    assert build_ledger(entities, covered_entity_ids=set()).slots[0].state == STATE_GAP_DISCLOSED
    assert build_ledger(entities, covered_entity_ids={"e1"}).slots[0].state == STATE_VERIFIED


def test_url_pattern_only_gap_gets_mismatch_note_but_doi_gap_does_not():
    entities = [
        _ent("u1", url_pattern="https://fda.gov/label/x", anchor="FDA label X"),
        _ent("d1", doi="10.1/d", url_pattern="https://x", anchor="Trial D"),  # has doi too
    ]
    led = build_ledger(entities, covered_entity_ids=set())
    by = {s.entity_id: s for s in led.slots}
    assert by["u1"].note and "canonical source" in by["u1"].note   # url_pattern-only -> note
    assert by["d1"].note == ""                                      # doi-bearing -> no note


def test_evidence_gaps_records():
    entities = [_ent("e2", severity="S0", s0_category="contraindications", anchor="X")]
    led = build_ledger(entities, covered_entity_ids=set())
    gaps = led.to_evidence_gaps()
    assert len(gaps) == 1
    g = gaps[0]
    assert g["entity_id"] == "e2" and g["severity"] == "S0"
    assert g["s0_category"] == "contraindications" and g["reason"] == "no_verified_citation"


def test_coverage_gaps_section_empty_when_no_gaps():
    entities = [_ent("e1", doi="10.1/a")]
    led = build_ledger(entities, covered_entity_ids={"e1"})
    assert render_coverage_gaps_section(led) == ""   # byte-identical OFF/no-gap path


def test_coverage_gaps_section_is_public_prose_no_internal_wording():
    entities = [
        _ent("e2", anchor="Trial B", doi="10.1/b"),
        _ent("u1", anchor="FDA label X", url_pattern="https://fda.gov/x"),
    ]
    led = build_ledger(entities, covered_entity_ids=set())
    out = render_coverage_gaps_section(led)
    assert out.startswith("## Coverage gaps")
    assert "Trial B" in out and "FDA label X" in out
    assert "not verified in this run" in out
    assert "canonical source" in out                  # the url_pattern note surfaces
    # no raw internal artifact-path wording (Codex design-gate P2)
    for banned in ("FRAME_GAP", "compose_gap_payload", "_GAP_STUB", "kept_sentences",
                   "strict_verify", "evidence_id"):
        assert banned not in out
    # NEVER fills a gap with a claim — it only discloses absence
    assert "verified citation" in out


 succeeded in 12687ms:
"""I-perm-021 (#1213) — RequiredEntityLedger: report-level required-entity completeness
accounting + honest gap disclosure (Codex design-gate APPROVE; narrow scope).

The completeness gap is largely UPSTREAM (retrieval/extraction); a reduce-time/report-level
ledger CANNOT manufacture coverage. Its job, per the Codex design ruling, is the NARROW
"inclusion + disclosure" surface (NO second LLM generation / recovery round — that is a
deferred follow-up):

  - Phase B (THIS module, report-level, POST-strict_verify): given the pre-registered native
    `required_entities` and the set of entity ids that earned a VERIFIED binding (the UNION of
    every VERIFIED claim's ``covered_element_ids`` from
    ``native_gate_b_inputs.build_native_gate_b_inputs`` — the EXACT same coverage computation,
    reused, never re-implemented), mark each required slot VERIFIED or GAP_DISCLOSED and emit
    an HONEST, DETERMINISTIC, TEMPLATED disclosure (no LLM, no fabricated citation).

§-1.1 SAFETY: this module assigns NO verdicts and adds NO coverage CREDIT. VERIFIED is set
ONLY from the caller's already-computed verified-binding set (which is itself gated by
strict_verify + the 4-role ``verdict==VERIFIED`` rule). It never touches strict_verify / the
4-role evaluator / D8 / the release decision. A gap disclosure is a templated "we could not
verify X" statement — it NEVER fills the gap with an unsupported claim.

Required entities come ONLY from the native scope template (the contamination lock — never
``outputs/dr_benchmark/`` / the gold rubric). The caller reads ``PG_REQUIRED_ENTITY_LEDGER``
at CALL TIME (default OFF, byte-identical when off); this pure module is simply not invoked
when the flag is off.
"""
from __future__ import annotations

from dataclasses import dataclass, field

# ── slot state machine ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# (Phase A states RETRIEVED/MAPPED are produced by the pre-gen retrieval feed, a separate PR;
#  this narrow disclosure module uses only the post-verify VERIFIED / GAP_DISCLOSED transition.)
STATE_MISSING = "missing"
STATE_RETRIEVED = "retrieved"
STATE_MAPPED = "mapped"
STATE_VERIFIED = "verified"
STATE_INCLUDED = "included"
STATE_GAP_DISCLOSED = "gap_disclosed"

# native required-entity dict keys (mirrors native_gate_b_inputs; read-only here).
_KEY_ID = "id"
_KEY_SEVERITY = "severity"
_KEY_ANCHOR = "anchor"
_KEY_RENDERING_SLOT = "rendering_slot"
_KEY_S0_CATEGORY = "s0_category"
# canonical identifier keys, in disclosure-preference order.
_CANONICAL_KEYS = ("doi", "pmid", "url_pattern")


@dataclass
class RequiredSlot:
    """One required entity's completeness state + the metadata needed to disclose it."""
    entity_id: str
    severity: str
    s0_category: str | None
    anchor: str
    rendering_slot: str
    canonical_ids: dict           # {doi?, pmid?, url_pattern?} (only present keys)
    state: str
    note: str = ""                # disclosure qualifier (e.g. url_mismatch); never a claim

    @property
    def is_url_pattern_only(self) -> bool:
        """True iff url_pattern is the ENTITY's only canonical id (no doi/pmid). Such an
        entity is structurally un-flippable by alternate-URL retrieval — coverage requires the
        VERIFIED claim to cite the exact canonical url_pattern (Codex design-gate q7)."""
        return "url_pattern" in self.canonical_ids and not (
            self.canonical_ids.get("doi") or self.canonical_ids.get("pmid")
        )


# Disclosure qualifier (Codex design-gate q7): public-facing, NOT raw internal artifact wording.
_URL_MISMATCH_NOTE = (
    "content for this topic may exist on an alternate source, but coverage remains unmet "
    "unless a verified claim cites the canonical source for this required entity"
)


@dataclass
class RequiredEntityLedger:
    slots: list[RequiredSlot] = field(default_factory=list)

    def verified_slots(self) -> list[RequiredSlot]:
        return [s for s in self.slots if s.state in (STATE_VERIFIED, STATE_INCLUDED)]

    def gap_slots(self) -> list[RequiredSlot]:
        return [s for s in self.slots if s.state == STATE_GAP_DISCLOSED]

    def coverage_fraction(self) -> float:
        return (len(self.verified_slots()) / len(self.slots)) if self.slots else 0.0

    def to_evidence_gaps(self) -> list[dict]:
        """Structured gap records for the manifest (machine-readable, audit trail)."""
        return [
            {
                "entity_id": s.entity_id,
                "severity": s.severity,
                "s0_category": s.s0_category,
                "anchor": s.anchor,
                "rendering_slot": s.rendering_slot,
                "reason": "no_verified_citation",
                "note": s.note,
            }
            for s in self.gap_slots()
        ]


def _canonical_ids(entity: dict) -> dict:
    return {k: entity[k] for k in _CANONICAL_KEYS if entity.get(k) not in (None, "")}


def build_ledger(
    required_entities: list[dict],
    covered_entity_ids: set[str] | frozenset[str] | list[str],
) -> RequiredEntityLedger:
    """Phase B: build the report-level ledger from the native required entities + the
    VERIFIED-binding set (``⋃ verified_claim.covered_element_ids``, computed by
    ``native_gate_b_inputs``). A required entity is VERIFIED iff its id is in
    ``covered_entity_ids`` (the exact existing coverage authority), else GAP_DISCLOSED.
    Assigns NO new credit; this is pure accounting + disclosure over an already-decided set."""
    covered = set(covered_entity_ids)
    slots: list[RequiredSlot] = []
    for entity in required_entities:
        entity_id = entity.get(_KEY_ID)
        if entity_id in (None, ""):
            # a config error elsewhere (validate_entity_severity is the fail-loud guard); skip
            # defensively here so the ledger never crashes on a malformed slot.
            continue
        canonical_ids = _canonical_ids(entity)
        verified = entity_id in covered
        slot = RequiredSlot(
            entity_id=str(entity_id),
            severity=str(entity.get(_KEY_SEVERITY, "")),
            s0_category=entity.get(_KEY_S0_CATEGORY),
            anchor=str(entity.get(_KEY_ANCHOR, "")),
            rendering_slot=str(entity.get(_KEY_RENDERING_SLOT, "")),
            canonical_ids=canonical_ids,
            state=STATE_VERIFIED if verified else STATE_GAP_DISCLOSED,
        )
        if not verified and slot.is_url_pattern_only:
            slot.note = _URL_MISMATCH_NOTE
        slots.append(slot)
    return RequiredEntityLedger(slots=slots)


def render_coverage_gaps_section(ledger: RequiredEntityLedger) -> str:
    """Deterministic, public-facing 'Coverage gaps' report section (NO LLM, NO fabricated
    citation, NO raw internal artifact wording — Codex design-gate q5 + P2). Returns "" when
    there are no gaps so the section is omitted entirely (and the OFF path stays byte-identical)."""
    gaps = ledger.gap_slots()
    if not gaps:
        return ""
    lines = [
        "## Coverage gaps",
        "",
        "The following pre-registered required topics could not be supported by a verified "
        "citation in this report. They are disclosed here rather than asserted without "
        "evidence:",
        "",
    ]
    for s in gaps:
        label = s.anchor or s.entity_id
        sev = f" ({s.severity})" if s.severity else ""
        note = f" — {s.note}" if s.note else ""
        lines.append(f"- **{label}**{sev}: not verified in this run{note}.")
    lines.append("")
    return "\n".join(lines)

  7127:             _seam_hb_live = [True]

  7132:                 # worker callback can NOT land a stale four_role_progress after the parent has cleared

   728: def run_four_role_seam(
   729:     transport: RoleTransport,
   730:     *,
   731:     run_dir: Path,
   732:     timestamp: str,

   735:     multi: object = None,
   736:     template: object = None,
   737:     slug: str | None = None,
   738:     domain: str | None = None,
   739:     ev_pool: object = None,
   740:     campaign_kg_db: str | Path | None = None,
   741:     heartbeat_claims_cb=None,
   742: ) -> FourRoleEvaluationResult:
   743:     """Resolve the 4-role inputs (builder WINS), run the SINGLE binding D8 gate, persist audit.
   744: 
   745:     This is the seam core extracted so BOTH the guarded `run_one_query` branch and the offline
   746:     seam test exercise the SAME code (no copy-paste of the override logic). Precedence (Codex
   747:     M3 P2 #1): if `four_role_input_builder` is provided it WINS — the SEAM calls it AFTER
   748:     generation with the run-local objects (`multi`, `template`, `slug`, `domain`, `ev_pool`) so
   749:     it PRODUCES the inputs+audit bundle from the finished report, and the SEAM writes
   750:     `bundle.audit_map` to `run_dir / FOUR_ROLE_CLAIM_AUDIT_FILENAME` (json, sorted keys) so every
   751:     claim_id is traceable alongside the run. Otherwise a directly-supplied static
   752:     `four_role_inputs` is used as-is (unit/static path; it carries no audit_map, so nothing is
   753:     written). If BOTH are None the branch fails closed (the sweep never synthesizes inputs).
   754: 
   755:     The run-local objects are passed through (NOT captured by the closure at construction)
   756:     because `multi`/`ev_pool` only exist inside `run_one_query` after generation; the builder
   757:     cannot have closed over them when the caller constructed it. Duck-typed `object` here so this
   758:     seam never imports the generator's `MultiSectionResult` (LAW VII CLI isolation).
   759: 
   760:     Pure orchestration over the INJECTED `transport` (no network, no spend) plus one JSON write.
   761:     """
   762:     if four_role_input_builder is not None:
   763:         # BUILDER WINS: produce the inputs+audit bundle from the finished report + native
   764:         # contract (supplied the run-local objects HERE), then run the gate over bundle.inputs.
   765:         bundle = four_role_input_builder(
   766:             multi=multi,
   767:             template=template,
   768:             slug=slug,
   769:             domain=domain,
   770:             ev_pool=ev_pool,
   771:         )
   772:         inputs = bundle.inputs
   773:         result = run_four_role_evaluation(
   774:             transport,
   775:             claims=inputs.claims,
   776:             run_dir=run_dir,
   777:             timestamp=timestamp,
   778:             coverage_ledger=inputs.coverage_ledger,
   779:             required_s0_categories=inputs.required_s0_categories,
   780:             model_slugs=inputs.model_slugs,
   781:             rewrite_already_attempted=inputs.rewrite_already_attempted,
   782:             campaign_kg_db=campaign_kg_db,
   783:             heartbeat_claims_cb=heartbeat_claims_cb,
   784:         )
   785:         # The SEAM (not the builder) persists the per-claim audit map alongside the run.
   786:         (run_dir / FOUR_ROLE_CLAIM_AUDIT_FILENAME).write_text(
   787:             json.dumps(bundle.audit_map, indent=2, sort_keys=True) + "\n",
   788:             encoding="utf-8",
   789:         )
   790:         return result
   791: 
   792:     if four_role_inputs is None:
   793:         raise ValueError(
   794:             "run_four_role_seam: PG_FOUR_ROLE_MODE is on and a transport was injected, but "
   795:             "neither a four_role_input_builder nor static four_role_inputs was supplied; the "
   796:             "sweep does not synthesize them (fail-closed)."
   797:         )
   798: 
   799:     # Static path (no builder): use the caller-supplied inputs as-is (no audit_map to persist).
   800:     return run_four_role_evaluation(
   801:         transport,
   802:         claims=four_role_inputs.claims,

   716:                 if is_s0 and s0_category is not None:
   717:                     covered_s0_categories.append(s0_category)
   718: 
   719:             # I-perm-020 (#1212): S0 coverage binder. AFTER per-claim verification (these are the
   720:             # strict_verify-VERIFIED sentences, `verification.is_verified` is the loop guard above),
   721:             # credit a required S0 SAFETY category whose entity this VERIFIED claim satisfies via the
   722:             # FULL I-perm-002 conjunction (canonical evidence match + population anchor +
   723:             # contraindication DIRECTION + negation guard, semantic recognition forced ON inside the
   724:             # binder). Fixes the measured drb_76 false hold (a faithful "not recommended for the
   725:             # immunocompromised" contraindication that the literal-token era left un-credited). DEFAULT
   726:             # OFF: the `PG_S0_COVERAGE_BINDER` flag is read at CALL TIME here (never at import); when OFF
   727:             # the binder module is NEVER imported and NEVER called, so `covered_s0_categories` /
   728:             # `covered_element_ids` / `best_rank` are byte-identical to legacy. The credit is an
   729:             # idempotent set-UNION (harmless if the existing literal path or
   730:             # PG_SWEEP_SEMANTIC_CONTRAINDICATION already credited the same category) and is STILL gated
   731:             # downstream by the 4-role `verdict==VERIFIED` check in release_policy — additive credit, NOT
   732:             # a gate relaxation. The D8 threshold and the release rule are untouched. A bound element is
   733:             # an S0 entity by construction, so it also raises `best_rank` to S0 (a claim that earns an S0
   734:             # category is an S0 claim — keeping severity coherent with s0_categories, exactly as the
   735:             # native loop above promotes severity when it covers an S0 entity).
   736:             if _s0_coverage_binder_enabled():
   737:                 from src.polaris_graph.roles.coverage_binder import bind_s0_coverage
   738: 
   739:                 bound_categories, bound_element_ids = bind_s0_coverage(
   740:                     claim_text=sentence,
   741:                     claim_evidence_records=records,
   742:                     validated_entities=validated,
   743:                 )
   744:                 for category in bound_categories:
   745:                     if category not in covered_s0_categories:
   746:                         covered_s0_categories.append(category)
   747:                 for element_id in bound_element_ids:
   748:                     if element_id not in covered_element_ids:
   749:                         covered_element_ids.append(element_id)
   750:                 if bound_element_ids:
   751:                     best_rank = max(best_rank, _SEVERITY_RANK[_SEVERITY_S0])
   752: 
   753:             claim_severity = next(
   754:                 sev for sev, rank in _SEVERITY_RANK.items() if rank == best_rank
   755:             )
   756:             s0_categories = sorted(set(covered_s0_categories))
   757: 
   758:             claims.append(
   759:                 FourRoleClaim(
   760:                     claim_id=claim_id,
   761:                     claim_text=sentence,
   762:                     evidence_documents=documents,
   763:                     severity=claim_severity,
   764:                     s0_categories=s0_categories,
   765:                     covered_element_ids=covered_element_ids,
   766:                 )
   767:             )
   768:             audit_map[claim_id] = {
   769:                 "section_index": section_index,
   770:                 "section_title": getattr(section, "title", ""),
   771:                 "sentence": sentence,

   773:                 "covered_element_ids": covered_element_ids,

   777: 
   778:     if not claims:
   779:         raise ValueError(

   781:             "evaluation over no claims cannot produce a release decision (fail-closed, "
   782:             "no vacuous input)."
   783:         )
   784: 
   785:     inputs = FourRoleEvaluationInputs(

   789:         model_slugs=model_slugs,
   790:         rewrite_already_attempted=False,

codex

   123:

   125:     then `text`. Empty text is NOT raised here — the builder's `_resolve_evidence` fails closed

   131:             return value.strip()
   132:     return ""
   133: 
   134:

   136:     """The record's full canonical source URL (verbatim), from `source_url` then `url`."""
   137:     for key in _RAW_SOURCE_URL_KEYS:
   138:         value = row.get(key)
   139:         if isinstance(value, str) and value.strip():
   140:             return value.strip()
   141:     return ""

   146: 
   147:     The greedy DOI body can absorb a publisher landing-page suffix (`/full`, `/pdf`, ...) or a
   148:     trailing punctuation mark lifted from prose. Both are deterministically trimmed so the
   149:     returned DOI is the bare canonical token that EXACTLY equals the entity's `doi` (P2 #4);
   150:     coverage stays fail-closed (a mis-trim simply fails to match — never over-credits).
   151:     """

   153:         if not text:
   154:             continue
   155:         match = _DOI_RE.search(text)
   156:         if not match:
   157:             continue

   160:             if doi.endswith(suffix):

   962:     puts .env values into ``os.environ`` BEFORE this slate runs, so a conservative .env default
   963:     (e.g. ``PG_MOST_MAX_EVIDENCE=300``, ``PG_AGENTIC_WEB_PER_ROUND=6``) SURVIVED the setdefault and
   964:     silently throttled the benchmark below the slate. Fix: every numeric key is a **FLOOR** —
   965:     ``max(existing, slate)`` — so a HIGHER operator/.env value (more capability, e.g.
   966:     ``PG_LLM_TIMEOUT_SECONDS=600`` in .env) is KEPT, but a LOWER default is RAISED to full capability.

+"""I-perm-021 (#1213) — RequiredEntityLedger: report-level required-entity completeness
+accounting + honest gap disclosure (Codex design-gate APPROVE; narrow scope).
+
+The completeness gap is largely UPSTREAM (retrieval/extraction); a reduce-time/report-level
+ledger CANNOT manufacture coverage. Its job, per the Codex design ruling, is the NARROW
+"inclusion + disclosure" surface (NO second LLM generation / recovery round — that is a
+deferred follow-up):
+
+  - Phase B (THIS module, report-level, POST-strict_verify): given the pre-registered native
+    `required_entities` and the set of entity ids that earned a VERIFIED binding (the UNION of
+    every VERIFIED claim's ``covered_element_ids`` from
+    ``native_gate_b_inputs.build_native_gate_b_inputs`` — the EXACT same coverage computation,
+    reused, never re-implemented), mark each required slot VERIFIED or GAP_DISCLOSED and emit
+    an HONEST, DETERMINISTIC, TEMPLATED disclosure (no LLM, no fabricated citation).
+
+§-1.1 SAFETY: this module assigns NO verdicts and adds NO coverage CREDIT. VERIFIED is set
+ONLY from the caller's already-computed verified-binding set (which is itself gated by
+strict_verify + the 4-role ``verdict==VERIFIED`` rule). It never touches strict_verify / the
+4-role evaluator / D8 / the release decision. A gap disclosure is a templated "we could not
+verify X" statement — it NEVER fills the gap with an unsupported claim.
+
+Required entities come ONLY from the native scope template (the contamination lock — never
+``outputs/dr_benchmark/`` / the gold rubric). The caller reads ``PG_REQUIRED_ENTITY_LEDGER``
+at CALL TIME (default OFF, byte-identical when off); this pure module is simply not invoked
+when the flag is off.
+"""
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+from dataclasses import dataclass, field
+
+# ── slot state machine ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
+# (Phase A states RETRIEVED/MAPPED are produced by the pre-gen retrieval feed, a separate PR;
+#  this narrow disclosure module uses only the post-verify VERIFIED / GAP_DISCLOSED transition.)
+STATE_MISSING = "missing"
+STATE_RETRIEVED = "retrieved"
+STATE_MAPPED = "mapped"
+STATE_VERIFIED = "verified"
+STATE_INCLUDED = "included"
+STATE_GAP_DISCLOSED = "gap_disclosed"
+
+# native required-entity dict keys (mirrors native_gate_b_inputs; read-only here).
+_KEY_ID = "id"
+_KEY_SEVERITY = "severity"
+_KEY_ANCHOR = "anchor"
+_KEY_RENDERING_SLOT = "rendering_slot"
+_KEY_S0_CATEGORY = "s0_category"
+# canonical identifier keys, in disclosure-preference order.
+_CANONICAL_KEYS = ("doi", "pmid", "url_pattern")
+
+
+@dataclass
+class RequiredSlot:
+    """One required entity's completeness state + the metadata needed to disclose it."""
+    entity_id: str
+    severity: str
+    s0_category: str | None
+    anchor: str
+    rendering_slot: str
+    canonical_ids: dict           # {doi?, pmid?, url_pattern?} (only present keys)
+    state: str
+    note: str = ""                # disclosure qualifier (e.g. url_mismatch); never a claim
+
+    @property
+    def is_url_pattern_only(self) -> bool:
+        """True iff url_pattern is the ENTITY's only canonical id (no doi/pmid). Such an
+        entity is structurally un-flippable by alternate-URL retrieval — coverage requires the
+        VERIFIED claim to cite the exact canonical url_pattern (Codex design-gate q7)."""
+        return "url_pattern" in self.canonical_ids and not (
+            self.canonical_ids.get("doi") or self.canonical_ids.get("pmid")
+        )
+
+
+# Disclosure qualifier (Codex design-gate q7): public-facing, NOT raw internal artifact wording.
+_URL_MISMATCH_NOTE = (
+    "content for this topic may exist on an alternate source, but coverage remains unmet "
+    "unless a verified claim cites the canonical source for this required entity"
+)
+
+
+@dataclass
+class RequiredEntityLedger:
+    slots: list[RequiredSlot] = field(default_factory=list)
+
+    def verified_slots(self) -> list[RequiredSlot]:
+        return [s for s in self.slots if s.state in (STATE_VERIFIED, STATE_INCLUDED)]
+
+    def gap_slots(self) -> list[RequiredSlot]:
+        return [s for s in self.slots if s.state == STATE_GAP_DISCLOSED]
+
+    def coverage_fraction(self) -> float:
+        return (len(self.verified_slots()) / len(self.slots)) if self.slots else 0.0
+
+    def to_evidence_gaps(self) -> list[dict]:
+        """Structured gap records for the manifest (machine-readable, audit trail)."""
+        return [
+            {
+                "entity_id": s.entity_id,
+                "severity": s.severity,
+                "s0_category": s.s0_category,
+                "anchor": s.anchor,
+                "rendering_slot": s.rendering_slot,
+                "reason": "no_verified_citation",
+                "note": s.note,
+            }
+            for s in self.gap_slots()
+        ]
+
+
+def _canonical_ids(entity: dict) -> dict:
+    return {k: entity[k] for k in _CANONICAL_KEYS if entity.get(k) not in (None, "")}
+
+
+def build_ledger(
+    required_entities: list[dict],
+    covered_entity_ids: set[str] | frozenset[str] | list[str],
+) -> RequiredEntityLedger:
+    """Phase B: build the report-level ledger from the native required entities + the
+    VERIFIED-binding set (``⋃ verified_claim.covered_element_ids``, computed by
+    ``native_gate_b_inputs``). A required entity is VERIFIED iff its id is in
+    ``covered_entity_ids`` (the exact existing coverage authority), else GAP_DISCLOSED.
+    Assigns NO new credit; this is pure accounting + disclosure over an already-decided set."""
+    covered = set(covered_entity_ids)
+    slots: list[RequiredSlot] = []
+    for entity in required_entities:
+        entity_id = entity.get(_KEY_ID)
+        if entity_id in (None, ""):
+            # a config error elsewhere (validate_entity_severity is the fail-loud guard); skip
+            # defensively here so the ledger never crashes on a malformed slot.
+            continue
+        canonical_ids = _canonical_ids(entity)
+        verified = entity_id in covered
+        slot = RequiredSlot(
+            entity_id=str(entity_id),
+            severity=str(entity.get(_KEY_SEVERITY, "")),
+            s0_category=entity.get(_KEY_S0_CATEGORY),
+            anchor=str(entity.get(_KEY_ANCHOR, "")),
+            rendering_slot=str(entity.get(_KEY_RENDERING_SLOT, "")),
+            canonical_ids=canonical_ids,
+            state=STATE_VERIFIED if verified else STATE_GAP_DISCLOSED,
+        )
+        if not verified and slot.is_url_pattern_only:
+            slot.note = _URL_MISMATCH_NOTE
+        slots.append(slot)
+    return RequiredEntityLedger(slots=slots)
+
+
+def render_coverage_gaps_section(ledger: RequiredEntityLedger) -> str:
+    """Deterministic, public-facing 'Coverage gaps' report section (NO LLM, NO fabricated
+    citation, NO raw internal artifact wording — Codex design-gate q5 + P2). Returns "" when
+    there are no gaps so the section is omitted entirely (and the OFF path stays byte-identical)."""
+    gaps = ledger.gap_slots()
+    if not gaps:
+        return ""
+    lines = [
+        "## Coverage gaps",
+        "",
+        "The following pre-registered required topics could not be supported by a verified "
+        "citation in this report. They are disclosed here rather than asserted without "
+        "evidence:",
+        "",
+    ]
+    for s in gaps:
+        label = s.anchor or s.entity_id
+        sev = f" ({s.severity})" if s.severity else ""
+        note = f" — {s.note}" if s.note else ""
+        lines.append(f"- **{label}**{sev}: not verified in this run{note}.")
+    lines.append("")
+    return "\n".join(lines)
diff --git a/tests/polaris_graph/generator/test_required_entity_ledger_iperm021.py b/tests/polaris_graph/generator/test_required_entity_ledger_iperm021.py
new file mode 100644
index 00000000..765a6792

+++ b/tests/polaris_graph/generator/test_required_entity_ledger_iperm021.py
@@ -0,0 +1,91 @@
+"""I-perm-021 (#1213) — RequiredEntityLedger (narrow: inclusion + honest disclosure).
+
+Proves the ledger is pure accounting + honest disclosure over the ALREADY-computed
+verified-binding set: VERIFIED only when the entity id is in the covered set (no new credit),
+GAP_DISCLOSED otherwise; url_pattern-only missing entities get the canonical-mismatch note;
+the Coverage gaps section is deterministic public prose (no LLM, no fabricated citation) and
+EMPTY when there are no gaps (so the OFF path stays byte-identical).
+"""
+from __future__ import annotations
+
+from src.polaris_graph.generator.required_entity_ledger import (
+    STATE_GAP_DISCLOSED,
+    STATE_VERIFIED,
+    build_ledger,
+    render_coverage_gaps_section,
+)
+
+
+def _ent(eid, *, severity="S1", anchor="", rendering_slot="", **canon):
+    e = {"id": eid, "severity": severity, "anchor": anchor, "rendering_slot": rendering_slot}
+    e.update(canon)
+    return e
+
+
+def test_verified_and_gap_states():
+    entities = [
+        _ent("e1", doi="10.1/a", anchor="Trial A"),
+        _ent("e2", doi="10.1/b", anchor="Trial B"),
+        _ent("e3", pmid="123", anchor="Trial C"),
+    ]
+    led = build_ledger(entities, covered_entity_ids={"e1", "e3"})
+    by = {s.entity_id: s for s in led.slots}
+    assert by["e1"].state == STATE_VERIFIED
+    assert by["e3"].state == STATE_VERIFIED
+    assert by["e2"].state == STATE_GAP_DISCLOSED
+    assert {s.entity_id for s in led.verified_slots()} == {"e1", "e3"}
+    assert {s.entity_id for s in led.gap_slots()} == {"e2"}
+    assert round(led.coverage_fraction(), 4) == round(2 / 3, 4)
+
+
+def test_no_new_credit_a_missing_entity_stays_gap():
+    # §-1.1: the ledger never flips a slot to VERIFIED unless its id is in the covered set.
+    entities = [_ent("e1", doi="10.1/a")]
+    assert build_ledger(entities, covered_entity_ids=set()).slots[0].state == STATE_GAP_DISCLOSED
+    assert build_ledger(entities, covered_entity_ids={"e1"}).slots[0].state == STATE_VERIFIED
+
+
+def test_url_pattern_only_gap_gets_mismatch_note_but_doi_gap_does_not():
+    entities = [
+        _ent("u1", url_pattern="https://fda.gov/label/x", anchor="FDA label X"),
+        _ent("d1", doi="10.1/d", url_pattern="https://x", anchor="Trial D"),  # has doi too
+    ]
+    led = build_ledger(entities, covered_entity_ids=set())
+    by = {s.entity_id: s for s in led.slots}
+    assert by["u1"].note and "canonical source" in by["u1"].note   # url_pattern-only -> note
+    assert by["d1"].note == ""                                      # doi-bearing -> no note
+
+
+def test_evidence_gaps_records():
+    entities = [_ent("e2", severity="S0", s0_category="contraindications", anchor="X")]
+    led = build_ledger(entities, covered_entity_ids=set())
+    gaps = led.to_evidence_gaps()
+    assert len(gaps) == 1
+    g = gaps[0]
+    assert g["entity_id"] == "e2" and g["severity"] == "S0"
+    assert g["s0_category"] == "contraindications" and g["reason"] == "no_verified_citation"
+
+
+def test_coverage_gaps_section_empty_when_no_gaps():
+    entities = [_ent("e1", doi="10.1/a")]
+    led = build_ledger(entities, covered_entity_ids={"e1"})
+    assert render_coverage_gaps_section(led) == ""   # byte-identical OFF/no-gap path
+
+
+def test_coverage_gaps_section_is_public_prose_no_internal_wording():
+    entities = [
+        _ent("e2", anchor="Trial B", doi="10.1/b"),
+        _ent("u1", anchor="FDA label X", url_pattern="https://fda.gov/x"),
+    ]
+    led = build_ledger(entities, covered_entity_ids=set())
+    out = render_coverage_gaps_section(led)
+    assert out.startswith("## Coverage gaps")
+    assert "Trial B" in out and "FDA label X" in out
+    assert "not verified in this run" in out
+    assert "canonical source" in out                  # the url_pattern note surfaces
+    # no raw internal artifact-path wording (Codex design-gate P2)
+    for banned in ("FRAME_GAP", "compose_gap_payload", "_GAP_STUB", "kept_sentences",
+                   "strict_verify", "evidence_id"):
+        assert banned not in out
+    # NEVER fills a gap with a claim — it only discloses absence
+    assert "verified citation" in out
